 /**
  * Script 1: Intro: Kid Selection
  */

[0000] (40) cutscene();												// Start Cutscene
[0001] (60) cursorCommand( kModeKeypad )							// Keypad Mode
[0003] (0C) loadSound(1);
[0005] (53) lockSound(1);
[0007] (0C) loadSound(58);
[0009] (53) lockSound(58);
[000B] (1A) Var[97] = 3;											// Kid1 is Dave
[000E] (25) loadRoom(45);
[0010] (1A) Var[91] = 0;											// Clear 'Start' status
[0013] (2A) delay(60);
[0017] (14) print(255,"=1987 Lucasfilm Ltd. All rights reserved");	// 29 Year old copyright notice
[003D] (58) beginOverride();

[0044] (48) if (VAR_HAVE_MSG == 0) {
[0049] (2A)   delay(120);
[004D] (48)   if (VAR_HAVE_MSG == 0) {
[0052] (48)     if (Var[92] == 1) {									// One Kid Selected?
[0057] (14)       print(255,"      Please select two other kids.");
[0076] (**)     }
[0076] (48)     if (Var[92] == 2) {									// Two Kids Selected?
[007B] (14)       print(255,"      Please select one other kid.");
[0099] (**)     }
[0099] (**)   }
[0099] (**) }
[0099] (10) breakHere();

[00A4] (83)   doSentence(9,139,0);									// Yes

[00AB] (**) }

 /**
  * Script 2: Game: Save/Load
  */
script-2.dmp														
[0000] (40) cutscene();												// Start Cutscene
[0001] (60) cursorCommand( kModeKeypad )							// Keypad Mode
[0003] (32) setCameraAt(20);
[0005] (25) loadRoom(50);											// SaveGame Room
[0007] (1A) Var[108] = 0;											// Game: Save/Load Status = Insert save-load disk
[000A] (58) beginOverride();
[000E] (42) startScript(128);										// start Game: Save/Load Disk Check Script
[0010] (1A) Var[50] = 0;											// SaveLoad: Button Pressed = Null
[0013] (10) breakHere();
[0014] (08) unless (Var[50] != 0) goto 0013;						// Wait for button press
[0019] (10) breakHere();
[001A] (7C) VAR_RESULT = isSoundRunning(19);						
[001D] (48) unless (VAR_RESULT == 0) goto 0019;						// Wait for light beep to finish
[0022] (48) if (Var[50] == 3) {										// If 'Continue Playing' pressed
[0027] (18) } else {
[002A] (48)   if (Var[50] == 1) {
[002F] (62)     stopScript(128);									// If 'Save Game' pressed
[0031] (A2)     Var[90] = saveLoadGame(Var[50]);					// Save the game
[0034] (48)     if (Var[90] == 3) {
[0039] (18)       goto 0061;
[003C] (**)     }
[003C] (42)     startScript(128);									// start Game: Save/Load Disk Check Script
[003E] (**)   }
[003E] (48)   if (Var[50] == 2) {									// SaveLoad: Button Pressed = Load Game
[0043] (A2)     Var[90] = saveLoadGame(Var[50]);					// Load the game
[0046] (**)   }
[0046] (48)   if (Var[90] == 0) {
[004B] (1A)     Var[108] = 3;										// Game: Save/Load Status = game was saved
[004E] (**)   }
[004E] (48)   if (Var[90] == 1) {
[0053] (1A)     Var[108] = 1;										// Game: Save/Load Status = game disk is still in drive
[0056] (**)   }
[0056] (48)   if (Var[90] == 2) {
[005B] (1A)     Var[108] = 2;										// Game: Save/Load Status = disk does not contain valid save game
[005E] (**)   }
[005E] (18)   goto 0010;
[0061] (**) }
[0061] (62) stopScript(128);
[0063] (C0) endCutscene();											// End Cutscene
[0064] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END


 /**
  * Script 3: Verb: Defaults
  */
script-3.dmp															
[0000] (48) if (VAR_ACTIVE_VERB == 1) {								// If Open Pressed
[0005] (75)   printEgo("It doesn't seem to open.");
[001B] (48) } else if (VAR_ACTIVE_VERB == 9) {						// If Push
[0023] (18)   goto 002E;
[0026] (48) } else if (VAR_ACTIVE_VERB == 10) {						// If Pull
[002E] (75)   printEgo("I can't move it.");
[003D] (48) } else if (VAR_ACTIVE_VERB == 12) {						// If Read
[0045] (42)   startScript(50);										
[0047] (48)   if (Var[92] == 0) {									// 
[004C] (75)     printEgo("It's too dark to read.");
[0060] (18)   } else {
[0063] (75)     printEgo("There's nothing to read on it.");
[007E] (**)   }
[007E] (48) } else if (VAR_ACTIVE_VERB == 14) {						// If Pickup
[0086] (75)   printEgo("I can't pick that up.");
[0099] (18) } else {
[009C] (75)   printEgo("That doesn't seem to work.");
[00B4] (**) }
[00B4] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END


 /**
  * Script 4: Door: Open
  */
script-4.dmp															
[0000] (EF) if (!getState08(activeObject)) {						// if door closed
[0003] (D7)   setState08();											// open door
[0004] (1C)   startSound(8);										// door open sound
[0006] (**) }
[0006] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END


 /**
  * Script 5: Door: Close
  */
script-5.dmp															
[0000] (6F) if (getState08(activeObject)) {							// If door is open
[0003] (57)   clearState08();										// close door
[0004] (1C)   startSound(9);										// Sound Door Closing
[0006] (**) }
[0006] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END


 /**
  * Script 6: Game: Meltdown Timer
  */
script-6.dmp															
[0000] (AF) if (!getState08(130)) {										// if inner-door is closed
[0004] (2A)   delay(300);												// 	Wait 5 seconds
[0008] (08)   if (VAR_ROOM != 6) {										// 	Not in Pool Area
[000D] (08)     if (VAR_ROOM != 1) {									// 	 Not in Front of Mansion
[0012] (08)       if (VAR_ROOM != 44) {									// 	  Not in Welcome to Mansion
[0017] (08)         if (VAR_ROOM != 2) {								// 	   Not in Bottom of Pool
[001C] (08)           if (VAR_ROOM != 16) {								// 	    Not in Garage
[0021] (1C)             startSound(32);									// 		 Sound Alarm 1
[0023] (1C)             startSound(33);									// 		 Sound Alarm 2
[0025] (**)           }
[0025] (**)         }
[0025] (**)       }
[0025] (**)     }
[0025] (**)   }
[0025] (2A)   delay(300);												// Wait 5 seconds
[0029] (3C)   stopSound(33);											// Stop Alarm 2
[002B] (42)   startScript(41);											// Cutscene: Dr. Fred: Meltdown
[002D] (2A)   delay(7200);												// Sleep 2 minutes
[0031] (3C)   stopSound(32);											// Stop Alarm 1
[0033] (2A)   delay(180);												// Sleep 3 seconds
[0037] (42)   startScript(57);											// Cutscene: Game Over
[0039] (**) }
[0039] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END

 /**
  * Script 9: Memoir: Reading
  */
script-9.dmp															
[0000] (48) if (Var[16] == 0) {											// if Memoir Quality == Terrible

[005C] (**) }

[0061] (75)   printEgo("This is the worst junk I've ever read.");
[0082] (**) }
[0082] (48) if (Var[16] == 2) {											// if Memoir Quality == Great
[0087] (75)   printEgo("This is great stuff!/The whole world should see it.");
[00B4] (**) }
[00B4] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END

 /**
  * Script 10: Memoir: Writing
  */
script-10.dmp														
[0000] (42) startScript(108);										// Typewriter: Actor Using
[0002] (10) breakHere();
[0003] (68) VAR_RESULT = isScriptRunning(108);						// Sleep until 'Typewriter: Actor Using' Finishes
[0006] (48) unless (VAR_RESULT == 0) goto 0002;
[000B] (48) if (VAR_EGO == 6) {										// If Wendy
[0010] (1A)   Var[16] = 2;											//  Memoir Quality = Great
[0013] (75)   printEgo("Ah! That's much better.");
[0029] (18) } else {
[002C] (1A)   Var[16] = 1;											//  Memoir Quality = Junk
[002F] (75)   printEgo("Whoops! I think I made it worse.");
[004B] (**) }
[004B] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END


 /**

  */

[0008] (2A) delay(180);												// Wait 3 seconds
[000C] (17) clearState08(53);										// Clear kObjectState_08 on Hamster
[000E] (8F) setState02(53);											// Set kObjectStateUntouchable on Hamster
[0010] (97) setState08(54);											// Set kObjectState_08 on Exploded Hamster			
[0012] (1C) startSound(16);											// Hamster Splat
[0014] (2A) delay(60);
[0018] (3C) stopSound(15);											// Microwave Sound
[001A] (1C) startSound(14);											// Microwave Bing
[001C] (A0) stopObjectCode();
END

 /**

  */

[000C] (2A) delay(60);
[0010] (2F) if (getState08(46)) {									// Window Broken?
[0014] (1C)   startSound(26);
[0016] (17)   clearState08(46);										// Crack Window
[0018] (**) }
[0018] (2A) delay(60);
[001C] (AF) if (!getState08(41)) {									// Chandelleer Broken?
